    USER: I wrote a sentence in English, but I'm not sure if it's grammatically correct. Here's my sentence: He washed yourself. 1. Are there any grammar mistakes in my sentence? Yes or No; 2. If yes, what is the category of the mistake: syntax, morphology or semantics ? If there's no mistakes, write 'None'
    ASSISTANT:
    1. Yes, there is a grammatical error in your sentence.
    2. The category of the mistake is syntax.
    3. The correct sentence should be "He washed himself."
EXPLANATION:
The verb "washed" agrees with the subject "he", but the object "yourself" does not agree with the verb. In English, we use reflexive pronouns like "himself/herself/itself" to indicate that the subject is performing an action on themselves. So, the correct sentence should be "He washed himself".
Therefore, there is a syntax error in your original sentence.
